Getting Started

1. Choose the integrations on the marketplace . After an approval you will see available integrations on the integrations page. In integration you will find the access tokens which should be used for development and production purposes. You can configure available options for each integration on the Integration page.

2. There are 2 options of using the integration:
  1. 1. iFrame integration
  2. 2. Direct link

3. Also, there is Swagger UI available for all the endpoints present in the system.

Discover it here:  https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/swagger.

iFrame integration

Secure face login and KYC integrations works as an iFrame integration on your website. To use the LaaS and Face KYC services simply insert the following code into your page. The iFrame would be initiated automatically and the user will be asked to use the fullscreen mode. If the user doesn't have a web camera on his device, he will have an ability to scan the QR code and proceed with his mobile phone. 

    <iframe
      src="FRAME_URL"
      allow="camera"
      allowfullscreen
    ></iframe>

Direct link

If you don't have a website but still want to use the Sahal Verifai you can simply redirect user to the link, which will be opened in the web browser tab
The user flow would be similar in this case.

Secure face login

Secure face login functionality contains of 2 parts:
  1. 1. User register
  2. 2. User login
User register
FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Secure face login integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/laas/face-register/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should be unique per user!

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification

User register is used to provide user ability to login into your application with face scan technologies.
Primary step is to create a unique reference for the user to let him use the platform across different devices. This identifier will be used to match users and to provide them access.

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • The FaceScan came from a Live Human and Liveness was Proven.
  • The Session Token was valid and not expired.
  • The Audit Trail Image came from the same Session as the FaceScan and the Audit Trail Image Matches the User in the FaceScan.
  • The FaceScan was not a replay.
  • The reference was a valid String and did not already exist in the Database.
  • The storage of the FaceMap to the Database succeeded without error.
User login
FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Secure face login integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/laas/face-login/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should exist in system

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification

User login is used to authenticate users into your application with face scan technologies.
To use this feature the user must be registered and have the personal identifier which will be used on login

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • The FaceScan came from a Live Human and Liveness was Proven.
  • The Session Token was valid and not expired.
  • The Audit Trail Image came from the same Session as the FaceScan and the Audit Trail Image Matches the User in the FaceScan.
  • The FaceScan was not a replay.
  • The reference was a valid String and already exists in the Database.
  • The FaceScan was Matched against a Liveness-Proven 3D FaceMap from the Database and Matched at Match Level 10.
  • A Continuous Learning FaceMap was produced and stored in the Database.

Facial biometric KYC

FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Facial biometric KYC integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/face-kyc/face-register/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should be unique per user!

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification

Facial biometric KYC is used to confirm the user personality.
During this check the user will be asked to scan his face and personal id.

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • A 3D FaceMap (where Liveness was already Proven) was used.
  • The reference was a valid String and already exists in the Database.
  • The 3D FaceMap was Matched against the ID Scan at minMatchLevel or greater.
  • The FullIDStatus was FullID. If the FullIDStatus was not FullID indicates the User needs to perform another scan.
  • The DigitalIDSpoofStatus was Physical ID. If the DigitalIDSpoofStatus was not Physical ID then this does not necessarily indicate the ID Scan was a Spoof. It could also indicate the User provided a poor or incomplete scan of the ID. If the DigitalIDSpoofStatus was NeedsRetry but the idScanFrontImage looks like quality data from a Full ID, the User will likely succeed on Retry when they provide slightly better data.

Facial biometric KYC simplified

FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Facial biometric KYC simplified integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/face-kyc-simplified/face-register/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should be unique per user!

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification
To get the documents from finished verification you should do the next:
  1. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/face-kyc-simplified/documents/download?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier

Facial biometric KYC simplified is used to confirm the user personality. Regardless, the Facial biometric KYC user doesn't have to confirm the document's data, it's verified via the Document verifications .
During this check the user will be asked to scan his face and personal id. Document can be uploaded via user's camera or via file uploader.

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • A 3D FaceMap (where Liveness was already Proven) was used.
  • The 3D FaceMap was Matched against the 2D Image at minMatchLevel or greater.
Verification links for users could be generated on the verifications page. You should use a unique reference per user to generate the link. Although you can configure the link expiration time, to let users use this link for the specific time period. The redirect link is optional and after success users will be redirected there.

Sahal Live Capture

FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Sahal Live Capture integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/sahal-live-capture/face-register/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should be unique per user!

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification
    3. full_registration: boolean, if false then the user will be asked to scan the face, complete the liveness check without any further steps. If true then the user will proceed to the full registration flow. It is true by default.

Sahal Live Capture is used to match users liveliness capture to his selfie photo

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • A 3D FaceMap (where Liveness was already Proven) was used.
  • The 3D FaceMap was Matched against the 2D Image at minMatchLevel or greater.

Digital signature

Digital signature functionality contains of 2 parts:
  1. Digital signature register
  2. Digital signature verify
Digital signature register
FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Digital signature integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/digital-signature/face-register/frame-url?reference=USER_REFERENCE&digital_signature=USER_FULL_NAME

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should be unique per user!
    And USER_FULL_NAME is a string that can be used to be shown as user signature

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification

Digital signature register is used to provide the user the ability to use his face scan as a digital signature.
Primary step is to create a unique reference for the user to let him use the platform across different devices. This identifier will be used to match users and to provide them access.
Second step is to use some user's information (i.e. his full name), to have his personal identifier.

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • The FaceScan came from a Live Human and Liveness was Proven.
  • The Session Token was valid and not expired.
  • The Audit Trail Image came from the same Session as the FaceScan and the Audit Trail Image Matches the User in the FaceScan.
  • The FaceScan was not a replay.
  • The reference was a valid String and did not already exist in the Database.
  • The storage of the FaceMap to the Database succeeded without error.

  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Digital signature integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route:

    Where USER_REFERENCE is the unique user identifier that will be attached to user face scan and will be used for matching on next requests.
    IMPORTANT! USER_REFERENCE should exist in system

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds
    2. redirect_url: url where user will be redirected after successful verification

Digital signature verification is used to let the user confirm his data(documents, photos, etc) in your application with face scan technologies.
To use this feature the user must be registered and have the personal identifier which will be used on verify

Success Criteria
success is true if ALL of the following are true:
  • The FaceScan came from a Live Human and Liveness was Proven.
  • The Session Token was valid and not expired.
  • The Audit Trail Image came from the same Session as the FaceScan and the Audit Trail Image Matches the User in the FaceScan.
  • The FaceScan was not a replay.
  • The reference was a valid String and already exists in the Database.
  • The FaceScan was Matched against a Liveness-Proven 3D FaceMap from the Database and Matched at Match Level 10.
  • A Continuous Learning FaceMap was produced and stored in the Database.

Video KYC

To get the Video KYC url you should send POST message with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 

  https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/video-kyc/conferences

The request body should contain the next fields: 

  {
    start_date: 'required|date|after_or_equal:now', // YYYY-MM-DD HH:ss
    end_date: 'required|date|after_or_equal:start_date', // YYYY-MM-DD HH:ss
    restrict_access: 'required|boolean',
    notes: 'nullable|string|max:5000',
    members: [{
      name: 'nullable|string|max:255',
      email: 'required|email',
      password: 'required|string|min:6|max:255',
      is_admin: 'required|boolean',
    }, {
      name: 'nullable|string|max:255',
      email: 'required|email',
      password: 'required|string|min:6|max:255',
      is_admin: 'required|boolean',
    }],
  },

Video KYC is used to connect 2 persons via the video chat.

Conference steps
  • After getting the conference url you can share it to the 2 persons
  • Users will lend on the login page where they must you the credentials you provided when requested the url
  • Then users will lend on the initial page with join conference button
  • After they're connected video session will start in limit of 240 seconds
  • The conference admin will be able to record the conference and then it will be available on the verifications page

Sahal KYC Portal

FRAME_URL is a link to the Sahal Verifai website, which handles the user's interaction. To get the url you can follow the next steps:
  1. Go to the integrations and choose the Sahal KYC Portal integration.
  2. Go to the Developers tab and copy the access token.
  3. Send a GET request with the Authorization header `Bearer YOUR_ACCESS_TOKEN` to the following route: 
      https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/full-kyc/verification-url

    You may also want to specify custom expiration time or whether it should be a full registration or only the liveness match. This can also be done via QUERY parameters:
    1. expiration_time: positive integer not less than 60, expiration_time time is seconds

Sahal KYC Portal contains multiple products above.
After creating the link and providing it to the user they will pass different steps which have the same events as other products.

Handling verification expiration When the verification is expired, you can provide the user with a similar link by putting a URID as the reference parameter 

  https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/full-kyc/verification-url?reference=URID

Usage

Handle iFrame events

When iFrame is injected into your page, the user will be suggested to open it in full screen mode. This will provide the best UX for the integration.

In your website you should listen for the message event. All the data will be passed via this channel. 
    window.addEventListener('message', YOUR_HANDLE_FUNCTION);
Structure of the message would be the next: 
    e: {
      data: {
        sahal: {
          success: true | false,
          data: ?CheckResults,
          error_message: ?string,
        },
      },
    };

If the check was invalid, the user will be offered to try again and will see the error message.
Error message will be presented in the window event, so you can handle it on your side.

In the success case you will receive the processed data and can handle it on your own.

Handle webhook events

When you are using a new tab feature the user will operate directly with the Sahal Verifai website.

The failed scenarios will be handled on our side to let the user proceed as soon as possible.

If webhooks are configured they will be sent on both fail and success scenarios with the results, so you can handle non-iFrame results.

Structure of the webhook payload could be the next:

Document verifications

Document verification API service is to process you to check and validate customers' identity documents on your website. Our technology becomes a part of your own backend.

Type of inspections

Visual

The Visual Inspection Zone (VIZ) of a Machine Readable Travel Document (MRTD) comprises the mandatory and optional data elements designed for visual inspection.

ICAO 9303 (2015).

MRZ

The Machine Readable Zone (MRZ) provides a set of essential data elements in a format, standardized for each type of a Machine Readable Travel Document (MRTD), that can be used by all receiving States regardless of their national script or customs. The data in the MRZ are formatted in such a way as to be readable by machines with standard capability worldwide.

ICAO 9303 (2015).

Image quality requirements

Below are the requirements for size and quality of document images captured by any device, which are necessary for successful image processing by Document Verification API:

  • Good lighting: Environment with good lighting helps with recognizing the characters in the image. When the image is too dark or too bright the document can not be validated.
  • Avoid reflections: Don’t use a flashlight on your device. Avoid reflections from lamps or environmental lights. Reflections on the image interfere with the processing and extracting the data.
  • Focus and sharpness: Make sure the image is clear and there are no blurred areas.
  • Angle: The tilt angle of the document should not exceed 10 degrees in any direction (horizontal or vertical).
  • Margins (too close): Make sure there’s minimum space around the document. Don’t zoom the image. It is recommended that the document takes up 70-80% of the image.
  • Margins (too far): Make sure the space around the document is not taking more than 20-30% of the image It is recommended that the document takes up 70-80% of the image
  • Contrast: The document should be in clear contrast to the background. A light-colored document on a light background, as well as a dark-colored document on a dark background, cannot be recognized.
  • Image resolution: To achieve good quality of recognition of identification documents, we recommend that you provide images captured by camera with a resolution of at least Full HD (1920×1080) and autofocus.
  • Subjection: Make sure your hands or other objects don’t cover document data.
Process:

Request:

Body     form-data

file       ../john-licence.jpg    or    base64 string 

    POST:

    https://demo.sahal.ai/api/v1/document-verification/process

An example of response JSON would be the next:

Results

After scanning process is completed, result will contain different result types: 

  └── document_type
  └── text_result
  └── graphic_result
  └── document_position
  └── barcode_position
  └── mrz_position
  └── image_quality_group
  └── overall_result
  └── authenticity_results
  └── rfid_sessionData
  └── chip_page
  └── resolution_type
  └── barcode_result
  └── processing_finished_status
  └── more_pages_available
  └── elapsed_time
  └── elapsed_time_rfid
  └── raw_result
  • document_type - document type result
  • text_result - text results
  • graphic_result - graphic results
  • document_position - position of document blank result
  • barcode_position - position of found Barcode result
  • mrz_position - position of the MRZ area
  • image_quality_group - image quality result
  • overall_result - it's a summary of all results, one of SLCheckResult enumeration values. If at least one result status was negative, overall result will be negative
  • authenticity_results - authenticity results
  • rfid_session_data - results of work with the SDK within the context of the current communication session with electronic document
  • chip_page indicates the presence and location of an RFID chip in a document. 0 - no rfid chip; 1 - chip is located in the document data page; 2 - chip is located in the back page or inlay of the document
  • resolution_type - it's an image resolution, one of ResolutionType enumeration values
  • barcode_result - barcode results
  • elapsed_time indicates how much time has been required for document processing, milliseconds
  • elapsed_time_rfid indicates how much time has been required for RFID chip processing, milliseconds
  • raw_result - contains results in the initial view, i.e. the raw view

Document Type Result 

└── name
└── document_id
└── i_c_a_o_code
└── f_d_s_i_d
└── d_type
└── d_format
└── d_m_r_z
└── d_description
└── d_year
└── d_country_name
└── page_index
  • name - Document type name
  • document_id - Document type numeric code
  • i_c_a_o_code - Document issuing country ICAO Code
  • f_d_s_i_d - Array of IRS document identifiers
  • d_type - Document type, one of DiDocType enumeration values
  • d_format - Document format, one of SLDocFormat enumeration values
  • d_m_r_z - Flag for MRZ presence on document
  • d_description - Document description text
  • d_year - Document issue year
  • d_country_name - Document issuing country name
  • page_index - Indicates an index of the document page, whence the result is received

Graphic Result 

graphic_result
└── fields
|   └── source_type
|   └── field_type
|   └── field_name
|   └── bound_rect
|   └── value
|   └── light_type
|   └── light_name
|   └── page_index
  • source_type - Identifies zone whence data was extracted. SLResultType class contains enumeration values
  • field_type - Field logical type, one of SLGraphicFieldType values. Enumeration contains identifiers determining the logical type of the graphic data obtained while reading document filling fields or barcodes
  • field_name - Title of the fieldType
  • bound_rect - Field rectangular area coordinates on the image (for document filling fields reading results visualOCRExtended (SLResultType enumeration))
  • value - Value which was obtained
  • light_type - Light type, one of SLGraphicFieldLight values. Enumeration contains a set of identifiers used for identifying document reader possibilities, specifying lighting schemes for scanning etc.
  • light_name - Title of the lightType
  • page_index - Indicates an index of the document page, whence the result is received

Image Quality Group 

image_quality
└── count
└── result
└── image_quality_list
|   └── type
|   └── result
|   └── feature_type
|   └── bound_rects
  • count - Number of results in the list
  • result - Overall check result, one of SLCheckResult enumeration values
  • image_quality_list - Array of single check result pointers, which contains:
    • type - check result type, one of SLImageQualityCheckType values
    • result - check result, one of SLCheckResult values
    • featureType - one of SLSecurityFeatureType values indicating the area examined
    • boundRects - coordinates of glares

Barcode Result 

barcode_result
└── fields
|   └── barcode_type
|   └── status
|   └── pdf417_info
|   |   └── error_level
|   |   └── columns
|   |   └── rows
|   └── data
|   └── page_index
  • barcode_type - Decoded barcode type, one of SLBarcodeType enumeration values
  • status - Indicates barcode reading result, one of SLBarcodeResult enumeration values or another value, which is SDK internal error code
  • pdf417_info - Contains the information about the PDF417 barcode, which includes the following parameters:
    • error_level - barcode error correction level
    • columns - number of columns in a barcode
    • rows - number of rows in a barcode
  • data - Results of reading data from barcode modules
  • page_index - Indicates an index of the document page, whence the result is received
